{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01G2bzmYvnfGGKx9tFBGhvS5","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"text","text":"## Complete Envoy Request Routing Flow Investigation\n\nI've successfully traced the complete path of an HTTP request through Envoy and created a comprehensive document at `/logs/agent/investigation.md`. Here's a summary of the findings:\n\n### **Q1: Listener Accept to Network Filter Chain**\n- **TCP Accept**: `TcpListenerImpl::onSocketEvent()` receives the socket via `accept()` system call\n- **ActiveTcpListener**: Routes the connection and decides whether to balance it to another handler\n- **Listener Filters**: `ActiveTcpSocket` iterates through listener filters (SNI inspection, TLS detection, etc.)\n- **Filter Chain Selection**: Once listener filters complete, `findFilterChain()` selects the appropriate filter chain based on connection properties (destination address, SNI, etc.)\n- **Server Connection**: `createServerConnection()` creates the downstream server connection with the selected transport socket\n\n### **Q2: HTTP Parsing and Filter Chain Iteration**\n- **Data Arrival**: `ConnectionManagerImpl::onData()` is called when bytes arrive\n- **Codec Creation**: HTTP codec (HTTP/1.1, HTTP/2, HTTP/3) is created lazily and parses the byte stream\n- **Stream Creation**: Codec calls `newStream()` callback, which creates an `ActiveStream` structure\n- **Filter Chain Creation**: `FilterManager::createDownstreamFilterChain()` instantiates all HTTP decoder filters (including router) and encoder filters\n- **Filter Iteration**: `FilterManager::decodeHeaders()` iterates through each decoder filter, allowing each to process and modify the request\n- **Filter Status Control**: Filters return `FilterHeadersStatus` to control iteration (`Continue`, `StopIteration`, etc.)\n\n### **Q3: Route Resolution and Upstream Selection**\n- **Route Selection**: `Router::Filter::decodeHeaders()` calls `callbacks_->route()` to match the request against route configuration based on virtual host, path, method, and other criteria\n- **Cluster Selection**: Once a route is matched, the route entry specifies the upstream cluster name via `route_entry_->clusterName()`\n- **Host Selection**: `cluster->chooseHost()` uses the configured load balancer algorithm (round-robin, least-request, etc.) to select a specific upstream host\n- **Connection Pool**: `createConnPool()` creates or reuses a connection pool for that specific host\n- **Upstream Stream Request**: `conn_pool_->newStream()` requests a stream from the connection pool, which either reuses an existing connection or creates a new one\n\n### **Q4: Upstream Connection and Data Flow**\n- **Connection Establishment**: Connection pool establishes TCP connection to upstream host, performs TLS handshake if needed\n- **Connection Ready Callback**: `onPoolReady()` is invoked with the upstream connection/stream\n- **Request Encoding**: Upstream filter chain passes request through filters ending at `UpstreamCodecFilter`, which encodes headers/data/trailers to wire format\n- **Socket Write**: Encoded data is written to the upstream TCP socket via the underlying `Network::Connection`\n- **Response Reception**: Codec receives response bytes, parses them, and calls `UpstreamRequest::decodeHeaders/Data/Trailers()`\n- **Response to Downstream**: Response flows back to router filter, through encoder filters, and is encoded by downstream codec to the client\n\n### Key Architectural Patterns:\n- **Layered Filtering**: Network filters (like HCM) → HTTP decoder filters → HTTP encoder filters\n- **Two-stage Codec Interaction**: One codec for downstream (receives bytes, produces streams), one for upstream (receives requests, produces bytes)\n- **Connection Pooling**: Upstream connections are pooled and reused across multiple requests\n- **Load Balancing**: Happens at the host selection stage, allowing sophisticated algorithms based on metadata, hashing, etc.\n\nThe complete documentation with specific file paths, line numbers, and class references is available in `/logs/agent/investigation.md`."}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":5,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1210,"cache_read_input_tokens":94156,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1210},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b52ed7fe-f1a4-4c3e-b33c-15dd52724143","uuid":"75f788f5-fbee-488d-ae46-1de97d60454a"}
